  28 |     }

  32 |     }

  39 |     }

  42 |         const layoutRandomIndex = Math.floor(Math.random() * 2) + 1;

  44 |         this.selectedLayout = await this.ctbLayout.selectOption({ index: layoutRandomIndex })
  45 |     }
